30, 2019|access-date=December 31, 2019|magazine=[[Forbes]]|url-status=live}}</ref>

Swift has invested in a real estate portfolio worth $84 million. In Nashville, she purchased a condo for $1.99 million in 2009 and a suburban [[Greek Revival architecture|Greek-revival]] estate for $2.5 million in 2011. In [[Beverly Hills, California|Beverly Hills]], California, she bought a $3.55 million [[Cape Cod (house)|Cape Cod-style]] cottage in 2011 and a $1.78 million single-story [[Mid-century modern|mid-century]] home in 2012; Swift sold both properties in 2018 for $4 million and $2.65 million, respectively. She purchased the [[Samuel Goldwyn Estate]], a [[Georgian architecture|Georgian-revival]] house in Beverly Hills, for $25 million in 2015, which she has since restored to its original condition. The estate was granted [[National Historic Landmark]] status in 2017<ref name="Real Estate"/> and contains Swift's [[home studio]], Kitty Committee, where she recorded songs for ''Folklore''.<ref>{{cite news|last1=Rosen|first1=Jody|date=July 24, 2020|title=Review: Taylor Swift's radically intimate 'Folklore' is the perfect quarantine album|work=Los Angeles Times|url=https://www.latimes.com/entertainment-arts/music/story/2020-07-24/taylor-swift-folklore-album-review|access-date=October 30, 2021}}</ref> In 2013, Swift acquired the [[Holiday House (Watch Hill)|Holiday House]], a seafront mansion in [[Watch Hill, Rhode Island]], for $17.75 million; she previously hosted annual [[Independence Day (United States)|Fourth-of-July]] parties on the estate and has had stalking incidents there.<ref name="Real Estate"/> In 2015, [[Gina Raimondo]], then-Governor of Rhode Island, proposed but never implemented a statewide property tax for second homes worth more than $1 million, dubbed the "Taylor Swift tax".<ref>{{Cite magazine|date=March 18, 2015|title='Taylor Swift Tax' Defended by Rhode Island Governor|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/news/6502525/taylor-swift-tax-rhode-island-governor|access-date=October 30, 2021|magazine=Billboard|language=en}}</ref> Holiday House also inspired Swift's 2020 song "[[The Last Great American Dynasty]]".<ref>{{Cite web|last=Suskind|first=Alex|date=December 9, 2020|title=Taylor Swift broke all her rules with 'Folklore' — and gave herself a much-needed escape|url=https://ew.com/music/taylor-swift-entertainers-of-the-year-2020/|access-date=December 9, 2020|website=[[Entertainment Weekly]]|language=EN|archive-date=March 12, 2021|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20210312063543/https://ew.com/music/taylor-swift-entertainers-of-the-year-2020/|url-status=live}}</ref> In New York City, her $47 million worth of property on a single block in [[Tribeca]] includes a $19.95 million duplex [[Penthouse apartment|penthouse]], an $18 million four-story [[townhouse]], and a $9.75 million apartment purchased in 2014, 2017 and 2018, respectively.<ref>{{cite web |last1=Yorio |first1=Janine |title=Is Taylor Swift A Brilliant Real Estate Investor? |url=https://www.forbes.com/sites/forbesrealestatecouncil/2019/05/07/is-taylor-swift-a-brilliant-real-estate-investor/?sh=16b05e702876 |website=Forbes |access-date=29 October 2021}}</ref><ref name="Real Estate"/>

=== Philanthropy ===
Swift is well known for her philanthropic efforts.<ref>{{Cite web|last=Aniftos|first=Rania|date=March 23, 2021|title=A Timeline of Taylor Swift's Generosity|url=http://www.billboard.com/amp/articles/news/8481430/timeline-taylor-swift-generosity|access-date=October 26, 2021|magazine=Billboard}}</ref> She was ranked at number one on [[DoSomething]]'s "Gone Good" list,<ref>{{Cite news|last=Couch|first=Robbie|date=March 2, 2015|url=http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2014/12/30/taylor-swift-charitable-celebrity_n_6391984.html|title=Taylor Swift Named Most Charitable Celeb For Supporting Feminist Causes, Education, More|work=[[HuffPost]]|access-date=August 2, 2016|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20161021170907/http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2014/12/30/taylor-swift-charitable-celebrity_n_6391984.html|archive-date=October 21, 2016}}</ref> and has received the "Star of Compassion" accolade from the Tennessee Disaster Services,<ref>{{cite web|url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-star-of-compassion-award/|title=Taylor Swift Receives Star of Compassion Award|work=[[Taste of Country]]|date=June 13, 2012|access-date=November 27, 2015|last=Pacella|first=Megan|url-status=dead|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20150713131701/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-star-of-compassion-award/|archive-date=July 13, 2015}}</ref> The Big Help Award from the [[Nickelodeon Kids' Choice Awards]] for her "dedication to helping others" as well as "inspiring others through action",<ref>{{cite web|url=http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-kids-choice-awards-michelle-obama/|title=Taylor Swift to Receive 'Big' Honor From Michelle Obama at Kids' Choice Awards|work=[[Taste of Country]]|last=Cooper|first=Brittany Joy|date=March 27, 2012|access-date=August 30, 2012|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20120712004900/http://tasteofcountry.com/taylor-swift-kids-choice-awards-michelle-obama/|archive-date=July 12, 2012}}</ref> and the Ripple of Hope Award for her "dedication to advocacy at such a young age".<ref>{{Cite news|url=http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/taylor-swift-honored-with-rfk-centers-ripple-of-hope-award-182081831.html|title=Taylor Swift Honored With RFK Center's Ripple of Hope Award|date=December 4, 2012|agency=[[PR Newswire]]|access-date=February 25, 2013|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20130507092910/http://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/taylor-swift-honored-with-rfk-centers-ripple-of-hope-award-182081831.html|archive-date=May 7, 2013}}</ref> In 2008, she donated $100,000 to the Red Cross to help the victims of the [[Iowa flood of 2008|Iowa flood]].<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.people.com/people/article/0,,20218079,00.html|title=Taylor Swift donates $100,000 to victims of Iowa Flood|last=Lee|first=Ken|date=August 9, 2009|work=[[People (magazine)|People]]|access-date=September 9, 2009|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20090607053519/http://www.people.com/people/article/0%2C%2C20218079%2C00.html|archive-date=June 7, 2009}}</ref> Swift has performed at charity relief events, including Sydney's [[Sound Relief]] concert.<ref>{{Cite news|url=http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/kylie-leads-mega-star-mercy-mission/story-e6freuy9-1111119064914|archive-url=https://www.webcitation.org/6kliTEckz?url=http://www.dailytelegraph.com.au/kylie-leads-mega-star-mercy-mission/story-e6freuy9-1111119064914?nk=5c8836647fb32c61997354b33be91d9c-1474745260|archive-date=September 2009|url-status=dead}}</ref> She recorded the song "Breathless" for ''[[Hope for Haiti Now (album)|Hope for Haiti Now]]'', a 2010 live album by various artists to alleviate the [[2010 Haiti earthquake]].<ref>{{cite web|last=Vena|first=Jocelyn|url=http://www.mtv.com/news/1630485/better-than-ezra-honored-by-taylor-swifts-performance-of-breathless-at-haiti-telethon/|title=Better Than Ezra 12, 2014}}</ref> In response to the [[May 2010 Tennessee floods]], Swift donated $500,000 during a telethon hosted by [[WSMV-TV|WSMV]].<ref name="Talbottflood">{{cite web|url=http://cnsnews.com/news/article/taylor-swift-donates-500000-nashville-flood-relief|date=May 7, 2010|last=Talbott|first=Chris|title=Taylor Swift Donates $500,000 to Nashville Flood Relief|work=[[CNS News]]|url-status=dead|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20151208160159/http://cnsnews.com/news/article/taylor-swift-donates-500000-nashville-flood-relief|archive-date=December 8, 2015}}</ref> In 2011, Swift used a dress rehearsal of her Speak Now tour as a benefit concert for victims of [[2011 Super Outbreak|recent tornadoes]] in the U.S., raising more than $750,000.<ref>{{Cite news|last=Lewis|first=Randy|title=Taylor Swift benefit concert raises more than $750,000 for tornado Swift is a supporter of the arts. 2015}}</ref> In 2012, she pledged $4&nbsp;million to fund the building of a new education center at the [[Country Music Hall of Fame and Museum]] in Nashville.<ref>{{Cite 5, 2012}}</ref> That year, she also partnered with textbook rental company [[Chegg]] to donate $60,000 to the music departments of six U.S. colleges.<ref>{{cite === Politics and activism ===
Swift is a [[Feminism|feminist]]<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/aug/23/taylor-swift-shake-it-off|title=Taylor Swift: 'Sexy? Not on my radar'|last=Hoby|first=Hermione|date=August 23, 2014|work=[[The Guardian]]|access-date=May 29, 2015|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20150610104506/http://www.theguardian.com/music/2014/aug/23/taylor-swift-shake-it-off|archive-date=June 10, 2015}}</ref> and [[pro-choice]].<ref name="GuardianInterview2019">{{cite news|url=https://www.theguardian.com/music/2019/aug/24/taylor-swift-pop-music-hunger-games-gladiators?|title=Taylor Swift: 'Pop music can feel like it's The Hunger Games, and like we're gladiators'|last=Snapes|first=Laura|newspaper=[[The Guardian]]|date=August 24, 2019|access-date=August 24, 2019|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20190824114530/https://www.theguardian.com/music/2019/aug/24/taylor-swift-pop-music-hunger-games-gladiators|archive-date=August 24, 2019|url-status=live}}</ref> She has been regarded as a feminist icon by various publications.<ref>{{cite web|last=Gallo|first=Mia|url=http://udreview.com/feminist-icon-taylor-swift-has-fought-misogyny-her-entire-career/|title=Feminist icon Taylor Swift has fought misogyny her entire career|date=February 23, 2021|work=The Review|access-date=April 3, 2021}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|last=Kilpatrick|first=Mary|url=https://www.cleveland.com/shatter/2018/07/why_taylor_swift_is_a_feminist.html|title=Why Taylor Swift is a feminist icon|date=July 17, 2018|publisher=cleveland.com|access-date=April 3, 2021}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|last=Armstrong|first=Jennifer Keishin|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/7423962/taylor-swift-feminism-impact|title=Taylor Swift's Feminist Evolution|date=July 1, 2016|work=Billboard|access-date=April 3, 2021}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|last=Ebbitt|first=Kathleen|url=https://www.globalcitizen.org/en/content/taylor-swift-is-my-feminist-hero/|title=Taylor Swift is my feminist hero|date=May 21, 2015|work=Global Citizen|access-date=April 3, 2021}}</ref> During the [[2008 United States presidential election]], she promoted the Every Woman Counts campaign, aimed at engaging women in the political process. She was one of many country stars to record a PSA for the Vote (For Your) Country campaign.<ref>{{Cite AV media|date=May 30, 2008|title=Every Woman Counts: Funny Taylor Swift Interview Before 2008 ACM Awards|url=https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MaJLtyYFiBQ|work=[[Lifetime (TV network)|Lifetime]]|access-date=August 2, 2016|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20101105043915/http://www.youtube.com//watch?v=MaJLtyYFiBQ|archive-date=November 5, 2010}}</ref> At the 2019 [[Billboard Women in Music|''Billboard'' Women in Music]] summit, where she was honored, Swift spoke out against sexism and [[misogyny]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.elle.com/uk/life-and-culture/culture/a30218896/taylor-swift-speech-feminism-award-scooter-braun/|title=Taylor Swift Just Delivered Her Most Feminist, Badass Speech Yet And We're Giving It A Standing Ovation|last=O'Malley|first=Katie|website=Elle|date=December 13, 2019|access-date=July 27, 2020}}</ref> She was one of the founding signatories of the [[Time's Up (organization)|Time's Up]] movement against sexual harassment.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://timesupnow.org/times-up-the-300-original-signatories/|title=The Original 300+ Time's Up Signatories|website=Time's Up|date=October 21, 2019|access-date=May 20, 2020}}</ref> Swift has also spoken out against LGBT discrimination.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/newsbeat-44352519|title=Taylor Swift sends 'love' and 'respect' to LGBT fans|work=[[BBC News]]|date=June 4, 2018|access-date=December 15, 2018|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181114063244/https://www.bbc.com/news/newsbeat-44352519|archive-date=November 14, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://slate.com/culture/2014/10/taylor-swift-welcome-to-new-york-new-song-from-1989-is-a-pro-gay-synth-pop-anthem.html|title=Taylor Swift's Pro-Gay "Welcome to New York" Takes Her Further Than Ever From Nashville|last=Wickman|first=Forrest|website=Slate|date=October 20, 2014|access-date=July 27, 2020}}</ref> Following the 2008 murder of openly gay teenager [[murder of Larry King|Larry King]], she recorded a [[Gay, Lesbian and Straight Education Network|GLSEN]] PSA aimed at combating [[hate crime]]s.<ref name="eonline1">{{cite web|url=http://uk.eonline.com/news/59855/portia-joins-ellen-to-stop-the-hate|title=Portia Joins Ellen To Stop The Hate|last=Malkin|first=Marc|date=March 10, 2010|work=[[E!]]|access-date=July 12, 2012|url-status=dead|archive-url=https://archive.today/20130122042055/http://uk.eonline.com/news/59855/portia-joins-ellen-to-stop-the-hate|archive-date=January 22, 2013}}</ref> The music video for Swift's anti-bullying song "Mean" deals in part with [[homophobia]] in high schools; it was nominated for an MTV VMA social activism award in 2011.<ref name="Hawgood 2010-11-05">{{Cite news|url=https://www.nytimes.com/2010/11/07/fashion/07ANTHEM.html|title=For Gays, New Songs of Survival|last=Hawgood|first=Alex|date=November 5, 2010|work=[[The New York Times]]|access-date=August 7, 2012|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20120609020459/http://www.nytimes.com/2010/11/07/fashion/07ANTHEM.html|archive-date=June 9, 2012}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=http://in.reuters.com/article/idINIndia-58624620110804|title=MTV adds social activism category to VMAs|date=August 4, 2011|work=[[Reuters]]|last1=Mayberry|first1=Carly|last2=Tourtellotte|first2=Bob|access-date=August 30, 2012|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20121012205523/http://in.reuters.com/article/2011/08/04/idINIndia-58624620110804|archive-date=October 12, 2012}}</ref> After the [[Orlando nightclub shooting]] in June 2016, Swift penned a letter to honor the victims.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.teenvogue.com/story/taylor-swift-posts-handwritten-message-to-families-of-orlando-victims|title=Taylor Swift Posts Handwritten Message to Families of Orlando Victims|last=Wiest|first=Brianna|website=Teen Vogue|date=June 18, 2016|access-date=July 27, 2020}}</ref> She encouraged support for the [[Equality Act (United States)|Equality Act]] in a letter addressed to Senator [[Lamar Alexander]] and a petition on [[Change.org]], which accumulated over 800,000 signatures and responses from the White House and various Democratic legislators.<ref>{{Cite Swift avoided discussing politics in her early career,<ref>{{cite news|last=Macsai|first=Dan|date=October 19, 2012|url=http://entertainment.time.com/2012/10/19/taylor-swift-on-going-pop-ignoring-the-gossip-and-the-best-worst-nickname-shes-ever-had/?iid=ent-main-lede|title=Taylor Swift on Going Pop, Ignoring the Gossip and the Best (Worst) Nickname She's Ever Had|work=Time|access-date=August 2, 2016}}</ref> but she has become politically active since the [[2018 United States elections]].<ref name="zimmerman" /> She has supported the [[March for Our Lives]] movement and [[Gun politics in the United States|gun control reform]] in the United States.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.businessinsider.com/taylor-swift-shares-support-for-gun-control-reform-in-instagram-post-2018-3|title=Taylor Swift Shares Support For Gun a Control Reform In Instagram Post|last=Lynch|first=John|website=Business Insider|date=March 23, 2018|access-date=May 20, 2020}}</ref> She endorsed candidates for public office for the first time ahead of the 2018 midterm elections, declaring her support for [[Democratic Party (United States)|Democrats]] [[Jim Cooper]] and [[Phil Bredesen]] to represent Tennessee in the [[United States House of Representatives|House of Representatives]] and [[United States Senate|Senate]], respectively.<ref name="zimmerman">{{cite news|author=Zimmerman, Amy|url=https://www.thedailybeast.com/taylor-swift-finally-got-political-why-now|title=Taylor Swift Finally Got Political. Why Now?|work=[[The Daily Beast]]|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181009012452/https://www.thedailybeast.com/taylor-swift-finally-got-political-why-now|archive-date=October 9, 2018|date=October 8, 2018|access-date=October 9, 2018}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|author=Parkinson, Hannah Jane|title=Taylor Swift finally makes a political intervention – will it sway voters?|url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2018/oct/08/taylor-swift-political-intervention-sway-voters-singer-vote-democrat-midterm-elections-millennials|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181008172804/https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2018/oct/08/taylor-swift-political-intervention-sway-voters-singer-vote-democrat-midterm-elections-millennials|archive-date=October 8, 2018|work=[[The Guardian]]|date=October 8, 2018|access-date=October 9, 2018}}</ref> In her endorsement, Swift expressed her desire for greater LGBT rights and gender and racial equality, condemned systemic racism, and encouraged her fans to vote according to their personal values.<ref>{{cite news|author=Buitrago, Juan|title=What about her reputation? Taylor Swift's political stance draws praise, backlash|url=https://www.usatoday.com/story/life/people/2018/10/08/taylor-swift-political-phil-bredesen-endorsement-marsha-blackburn/1563958002/|date=October 8, 2018|access-date=October 8, 2018|newspaper=[[USA Today]]|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181008135135/https://www.usatoday.com/story/life/people/2018/10/08/taylor-swift-political-phil-bredesen-endorsement-marsha-blackburn/1563958002/|archive-date=October 8, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref> In August 2020, Swift urged her fans to check their voter registration ahead of elections.<ref>{{Cite web|last=Jones|first=Valerie|date=September 8, 2020|title=Here's what Taylor Swift, Julianne Hough and other stars are doing to encourage people to register to vote|url=https://www.deseret.com/entertainment/2020/9/8/21428073/taylor-swift-julianne-hough-billie-eilish-just-vote-campaign-voter-registration-usher-dj-khaled|access-date=October 6, 2020|website=[[Deseret News]]}}</ref> [[Vote.org]] reported that 65,000 people had registered to vote within 24 hours of Swift's post, an unprecedented surge even accounting for usual registration increases as deadlines approach.<ref name="France18">{{cite news|last1=France|first1=Lisa Respers|title=Voter registration reportedly spikes after Taylor Swift post|url=https://www.cnn.com/2018/10/09/entertainment/taylor-swift-voter-registration/index.html|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181009194930/https://edition.cnn.com/2018/10/09/entertainment/taylor-swift-voter-registration/index.html|archive-date=October 9, 2018|access-date=October 9, 2018|work=[[CNN]]|date=October 9, 2018}}</ref><ref name="Haag18">{{cite news|last1=Haag|first1=Matthew|title=Voter Registrations Spike as Deadlines Loom. Taylor Swift Had Something to Do With It.|url=https://www.nytimes.com/2018/10/09/us/politics/taylor-swift-voter-registration.html|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20181009210812/https://www.nytimes.com/2018/10/09/us/politics/taylor-swift-voter-registration.html|archive-date=October 9, 2018|access-date=October 10, 2018|work=[[The New York Times]]|date=October 9, 2018}}</ref> She endorsed [[Joe Biden]] and [[Kamala Harris]] in the [[2020 United States presidential election]]<ref>{{Cite news|last=Stevens|first=Matt|date=October 7, 2020|title=Taylor Swift, leaning further into politics, endorses Joe Biden and Kamala Harris.|work=[[The New York Times]]|url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/10/07/us/politics/taylor-swift-joe-biden-kamala-harris.html|access-date=October 8, 2020|issn=0362-4331}}</ref> and was found to be one of the most influential celebrities in the polls.<ref>{{Cite magazine|last=Gardner|first=Chris|date=October 29, 2020|title=LeBron James, Taylor Swift Among Most Influential Celebrities In 2020 Election: Study|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/news/9474197/lebron-james-taylor-swift-influential-celebrities-2020-election-study|access-date=October 29, 2020|magazine=[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]}}</ref> She lent her song "[[Only the Young (Taylor Swift song)|Only the Young]]" for use in an advertisement to increase voter turnout.<ref>{{Cite magazine|last=Blistein|first=Jon|date=October 30, 2020|title=Taylor Swift Lends 'Only the Young' to New Political Ad|url=https://www.rollingstone.com/music/music-news/taylor-swift-lends-only-the-young-to-new-political-ad-1083987/|access-date=October 30, 2020|magazine=[[Rolling Stone]]}}</ref>

The companies acted as the official airlines for the Australian and Asian legs; [[Cornetto (ice cream)|Cornetto]] sponsored the Asian leg of the tour.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.campaignasia.com/BlogEntry/383987,Taylor+Swift+melts+Cornettos+brand+image+in+Asia.aspx|title=Taylor Swift melts Cornetto's brand image in Asia|publisher=Campaign Asia|type=Blog|last=Reed|first=Chris|date=November 25, 2015|access-date=December 3, 2015|url-status=dead|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20151206133519/http://www.campaignasia.com/BlogEntry/383987%2CTaylor%2BSwift%2Bmelts%2BCornettos%2Bbrand%2Bimage%2Bin%2BAsia.aspx|archive-date=December 6, 2015}}</ref> While promoting ''1989'', Swift had tie-ins with [[Subway (restaurant)|Subway]], [[Keds]], Target, [[Xfinity]], and Diet Coke.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6266355/meet-taylor-swift-subway-campaign|title=Taylor Swift|work=[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]|date=September 26, 2014|access-date=November 20, 2014|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20141129145212/http://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop-shop/6266355/meet-taylor-swift-subway-campaign|archive-date=November 29, 2014}}</ref> In 2014, Swift released her fifth fragrance, Incredible Things.<ref>{{cite web|last=Mychaskiw|first=Marianne|url=http://news.instyle.com/2014/10/01/taylor-swift-fragrance-incredible-things/|title=Taylor Swift Is Launching Her Fourth Fragrance!|work=[[InStyle]]|date=October 1, 2014|access-date=December 3, 2015|url-status=dead|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20150107132326/http://news.instyle.com/2014/10/01/taylor-swift-fragrance-incredible-things/|archive-date=January 7, 2015}}</ref> In 2016, she worked with [[Apple Music]] to release a series of three commercials.<ref>{{cite magazine|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/chart-beat/7377374/taylor-swift-apple-music-ads-sales-streaming-boost|title=How Taylor Swift's Apple Music Ads Helped Drake, Future, the Darkness and Jimmy Eat World|last=Rutherford|first=Kevin|magazine=Billboard|date=May 18, 2016|access-date=July 27, 2020}}</ref>

Swift signed a multi-year deal with [[AT&T]] in 2016.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.forbes.com/sites/hughmcintyre/2016/10/04/taylor-swift-has-signed-a-multi-year-deal-with-att/|title=Taylor Swift Has Signed A Multi-Year Deal With AT&T|last=McIntyre|first=Hugh|work=Forbes|access-date=September 11, 2018|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20180911045449/https://www.forbes.com/sites/hughmcintyre/2016/10/04/taylor-swift-has-signed-a-multi-year-deal-with-att/|archive-date=September 11, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref> She later headlined [[DirecTV]]'s ''Super Saturday Night'' event on the eve of the 2017 [[Super Bowl]]. While promoting ''Reputation'', Swift released a series of behind-the-scenes videos showing the album recording process through DirecTV.<ref>{{cite news|url=http://fortune.com/2016/10/04/taylor-swift-att-deal-super-bowl/|title=Taylor Swift Signed a 'Multi-Year' Deal with AT&T|work=[[Fortune (magazine)|Fortune]]|access-date=September 11, 2018|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20180911045144/http://fortune.com/2016/10/04/taylor-swift-att-deal-super-bowl/|archive-date=September 11, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref> In 2018, Swift released two commercials for AT&T.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.rollingstone.com/music/music-news/taylor-swift-spars-with-andy-samberg-steals-cookie-dough-in-promotional-video-205946/|title=Taylor Swift Spars With Andy Samberg, Steals Cookie Dough in Promo Video|last=Chen|first=Joyce|date=September 7, 2017|work=[[Rolling Stone]]|access-date=September 11, 2018|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20180911081555/https://www.rollingstone.com/music/music-news/taylor-swift-spars-with-andy-samberg-steals-cookie-dough-in-promotional-video-205946/|archive-date=September 11, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8453777/taylor-swift-rides-caticorn-directtv-now-commercial|title=Taylor Swift Rides a Magical Caticorn in DirectTV NOW Commercial|work=[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]|access-date=September 11, 2018|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20180911064556/https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8453777/taylor-swift-rides-caticorn-directtv-now-commercial|archive-date=September 11, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref> The same year, Swift partnered with [[United Parcel Service|UPS]] as an official delivery partner for ''Reputation''<ref>{{cite press release|url=https://www.pressroom.ups.com/pressroom/ContentDetailsViewer.page?ConceptType=PressReleases&id=1503657046045-509|title=UPS Is The Official Delivery Partner For Taylor Swift's 6th Studio Album reputation|location=Atlanta, Georgia|date=August 25, 2017|access-date=May 13, 2020}}</ref> and [[Fujifilm]] on a special-edition autographed [[Instax]] camera, which includes a selfie-mode and [[double exposure]].<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.billboard.com/articles/columns/pop/8471742/taylor-swift-instax-camera-videos|title=Taylor Swift Unveils Her Special-Edition Instax Camera: Watch the Videos|last=Mele|first=Sofia|date=August 22, 2018|work=[[Billboard (magazine)|Billboard]]|access-date=September 11, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnet.com/news/taylor-swift-teases-her-special-edition-instax-camera-in-three-videos/|title=Taylor Swift teases her special edition Instax camera in three videos|last=Collins|first=Katie|date=August 22, 2018|publisher=[[CNET]]|access-date=September 11, 2018|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20180911045042/https://www.cnet.com/news/taylor-swift-teases-her-special-edition-instax-camera-in-three-videos/|archive-date=September 11, 2018|url-status=live}}</ref> The cameras showed massive growth in sales after partnership with Swift.<ref name=":11">{{cite news|url=https://www.digitalcameraworld.com/news/fujifilm-instax-cameras-sales-hit-900000-a-month-thanks-to-taylor-swift|title=Fujifilm instax cameras sales hit 900,000 a month, thanks to Taylor Swift|last=Artaius|first=James|date=February 11, 2019|website=Digital Camera World|access-date=January 1, 2019}}</ref> In 2019, Swift signed a multi-year partnership with [[Capital One]],<ref>{{cite press release|url=https://www.prnewswire.com/news-releases/capital-one-announces-exclusive-partnership-with-10-time-grammy-award-winning-artist-taylor-swift-300891605.html|title=Capital One Announces [[sustainable fashion|sustainable clothing line]] with [[Stella McCartney]].<ref>{{cite web |last1=Yotka |first1=Steff |title=Taylor Swift and Stella McCartney Reveal Their Lover Fashion Collaboration
